\DoxyCodeLine{00944\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Flags\ that\ configure\ how\ the\ Builder\ behaves.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00945\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ "{}Share"{}\ flags\ determine\ if\ the\ Builder\ automatically\ tries\ to\ pool}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00946\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ this\ type.\ Pooling\ can\ reduce\ the\ size\ of\ serialized\ data\ if\ there\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00947\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ multiple\ maps\ of\ the\ same\ kind,\ at\ the\ expense\ of\ slightly\ slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00948\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ serialization\ (the\ cost\ of\ lookups)\ and\ more\ memory\ use\ (std::set).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00949\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ By\ default\ this\ is\ on\ for\ keys,\ but\ off\ for\ strings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00950\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Turn\ keys\ off\ if\ you\ have\ e.g.\ only\ one\ map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00951\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Turn\ strings\ on\ if\ you\ expect\ many\ non-\/unique\ string\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00952\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Additionally,\ sharing\ key\ vectors\ can\ save\ space\ if\ you\ have\ maps\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00953\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ identical\ field\ populations.}}
